data-ft="&#123;&quot;type&quot;:1,&quot;tn&quot;:&quot;K&quot;&#125;"> <span class="messageBody" data-ft="&#123;&quot;type&quot;:3&#125;">If you are thinking about repairs to your Hybrid, this is the place.  I called on Tuesday about replacing my battery, Andy gave me a quote and set up an appointment... And no the rest of the story.... I live in Dodge City Kansas and wanted to drive out, have the battery replaced and drive home.  I expected this to be a problem.  But no the people at Mile Hybrid Automotive got things set up, did the repair while I waited and put me back on the road, I was home by 8pm.
If I ever have another problem with my Hybrid this is where it will be fixed.
Thanks to Andy and all the guys that go me back on the road. Yes, those exist, I work in one in the Elyria-Swansea neighborhood of Denver. If you live in Elyria-Swansea, this box of food is $20.

What if I offered to bring it to Longmont if you ordered it?

Its easy, order and pay for it by Weds, pick it up on Sat. (or I can bring it to Longmont on Monday).

This is the work of our good friends and neighbors at The GrowHaus near MileHybrid Automotive/Adopt A Part in the Elyria-Swansea neighborhood in Denver.
